)@@G@@:@@@[,@]@@@@2DESCRIPTION:@@@[8@G@@@@  THIS IS A DEMAND PROCESSOR THAT ALEW
)@@G@@LOWS A UNISCOPE 100, 200, OR 400    :@@@]]@F@@@@ TO AVOID SYSTEM TIMEOUTEX
)@@G@@ UNTIL A SPECIFIED TIME. THE HOLD MAY BE  :@@@]G@G@@@@ TERMINATED AT ANYEY
)@@G@@ TIME BY ENTERING A CONTROL IMAGE. THIS IS UNLIKE     :@@@]Q@F@@@@ MOST EZ

)@@G@@:@@@AA@F@@@@ IF NO OPTIONS ARE SPECIFIED THEY WILL DEFAULT TO T. IF NO TFO
)@@G@@IME   :@@@AK@G@@@@ IS SPECIFIED, IT WILL DEFAULT TO 15 MINUTES FROM THE FP
